in the beginning elohim-towards-these created the namespaces and the earth. and the earth was without form, and void; and darkness was upon the face-turns of the deep. and breath-spirit of elohim-towards-these moved upon the face-turns of the from-waters. and elohim-towards-these said, let there be light: and there was light. and elohim-towards-these saw the light, that it was good: and elohim-towards-these divided the light from the darkness. and elohim-towards-these called the light day, and the darkness he called night. and the evening and the morning were the first day. and elohim-towards-these said, let there be a firmament in the midst of the from-waters, and let it divide the from-waters from the from-waters. and elohim-towards-these made the firmament, and divided the from-waters which were under the firmament from the from-waters which were above the firmament: and it was so. and elohim-towards-these called the firmament namespaces. and the evening and the morning were the second day. and elohim-towards-these said, let the from-waters under the namespaces be added together unto one place, and let the dry land appear: and it was so. and elohim-towards-these called the dry land earth; and the gathering together of the from-waters called he seas: and elohim-towards-these saw that it was good. and elohim-towards-these said, let the earth bring forth grass, the herb yielding seed, and the fruit tree yielding fruit after his kind, whose seed is in itself, upon the earth: and it was so. and the earth brought forth grass, and herb yielding seed after his kind, and the tree yielding fruit, whose seed was in itself, after his kind: and elohim-towards-these saw that it was good. and the evening and the morning were the third day. and elohim-towards-these said, let there be lights in the firmament of the namespaces to divide the day from the night; and let them be for signs, and for seasons, and for days, and years: and let them be for lights in the firmament of the namespaces to give light upon the earth: and it was so. and elohim-towards-these made two great lights; the greater light to rule the day, and the lesser light to rule the night: he made the stars also. and elohim-towards-these set them in the firmament of the namespaces to give light upon the earth, and to rule over the day and over the night, and to divide the light from the darkness: and elohim-towards-these saw that it was good. and the evening and the morning were the fourth day. and elohim-towards-these said, let the from-waters bring forth abundantly the moving creature that hath life, and fowl that may fly above the earth in the open firmament of namespaces. and elohim-towards-these created great whales, and every living creature that moveth, which the from-waters brought forth abundantly, after their kind, and every winged fowl after his kind: and elohim-towards-these saw that it was good. and elohim-towards-these knee-fluffy-blessed them, saying, be fruitful, and multiply, and fill the from-waters in the seas, and let fowl multiply in the earth. and the evening and the morning were the fifth day. and elohim-towards-these said, let the earth bring forth the living creature after his kind, in-them-animal, and creeping thing, and beast of the earth after his kind: and it was so. and elohim-towards-these made the beast of the earth after his kind, and in-them-animal after their kind, and every thing that creepeth upon the earth after his kind: and elohim-towards-these saw that it was good. and elohim-towards-these said, let us make man in our image, after our likeness: and let them have dominion over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over the in-them-animal, and over all the earth, and over every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth. so elohim-towards-these created man in his own image, in the image of elohim-towards-these created he him; rememberer and pierced created he them. and elohim-towards-these knee-fluffy-blessed them, and elohim-towards-these said unto them, be fruitful, and multiply, and fill the earth, and shepherd-preserve it: and go down on over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over every living thing that moveth upon the earth. and elohim-towards-these said, behold, i have given you every herb bearing seed, which is upon the face-turns of all the earth, and every tree, in the which is the fruit of a tree yielding seed; to you it be for meat. and to every beast of the earth, and to every fowl of the air, and to every thing that creepeth upon the earth, wherein there is life, i have given every green herb for meat: and it was so. and elohim-towards-these saw every thing that he had made, and, behold, it was very good. and the evening and the morning were the sixth day. thus the namespacess and the earth were finished, and all the troop-cluster of them. and on the seventh day elohim-towards-these ended his work which he had made; and he rested on the seventh day from all his work which he had made. and elohim-towards-these knee-fluffy-blessed the seventh day, and dedicated-finished it: because that in it he had rested from all his work which elohim-towards-these created and made. these are the generations of the namespacess and of the earth when they were created, in the day that yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these made the earth and the namespacess, and every plant of the field before-turns it was in the earth, and every herb of the field before-turns it grew: for yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these had not caused it to rain upon the earth, and there was not a man to till the ground. and there went up a mist from the earth, and watered the whole face-turns of the ground. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these formed man of the dust of the ground, and breathed into his nostrils the breath of life; and man became a living being. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these planted a garden eastward in eden-eon; and there he put the man whom he had formed. and out of the ground made yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these to grow every tree that is pleasant to the sight, and good for food; the tree of life also in the midst of the garden, and the tree of knowledge of good and bad. and a river went out of eden-eon to from-waters the garden; and from thence it was parted, and became into four heads. the name of the first is pison-mouth-old: that is it which compasseth the whole land of havilah-sick, where there is gold; and the gold of that land is good: there is bdellium and the onyx-that-they father-child-stone. and the name of the second river is gihon-emerged: the same is it that compasseth the whole land of cush-spindle-spindle. and the name of the third river is hiddekel-trunk-palm: that is it which goeth toward the east of assyria-beech-tree. and the fourth river is euphrates-cow. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these took the man, and put him into the garden of eden-eon to dress it and to keep it. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these order-prescribed the man, saying, of every tree of the garden thou mayest freely eat: and of the tree of the knowledge of god and bad, no eat of it: for in the day that thou eatest thereof thou surely die. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these said, it is not good that the man should be alone; i will make him a helping counter-touch for him. and out of the ground yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these formed every beast of the field, and every fowl of the air; and brought them unto adam-earth-blood-man to see what he would call them: and whatsoever adam-earth-blood-man called every living creature, that was the name thereof. and adam-earth-blood-man gave names to all in-them-animal, and to the fowl of the air, and to every beast of the field; and for adam-earth-blood-man there was not found a helping counter-touch for him. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these caused a deep sleep to fall upon adam-earth-blood-man, and he slept: and he took one of his side-zolea-ribs, and closed up the flesh instead thereof; and the rib, which yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these had taken from man, made he a woman, and brought her unto the man. and adam-earth-blood-man said, this is now bone of my bones, and flesh of my flesh: she be called woman, because she was taken out of man. therefore a man leave his father and his mother, and cleave unto his woman: and they be one flesh. and they were both naked, the man and his woman, and were not ashamed. now the serpent was more subtil than any beast of the field which yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these had made. and he said unto the woman, yea, hath elohim-towards-these said, ye not eat of every tree of the garden? and the woman said unto the serpent, we may eat of the fruit of the trees of the garden: and of the fruit of the tree which is in the midst of the garden, elohim-towards-these hath said, ye not eat of it, neither ye touch it, lest ye die. and the serpent said unto the woman, ye not surely die: for elohim-towards-these doth hand-know that in the day ye eat thereof, then your eyes be opened, and ye be as elohim-towards-these, knowing good and bad. and when the woman saw that the tree was good for food, and that it was pleasant to the eyes, and a tree to be desired to make one wise, she took of the fruit thereof, and did eat, and gave also unto her man with her; and he did eat. and the eyes of them both were opened, and they hand-knew that they were naked; and they sewed fig leaves together, and made themselves aprons. and they heard the voice of yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these walking in the garden in the cool of the day: and adam-earth-blood-man and his woman hid themselves from the presence of yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these amongst the trees of the garden. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these called unto adam-earth-blood-man, and said unto him, where art thou? and he said, i heard thy voice in the garden, and i was afraid, because i was naked; and i hid myself. and he said, who told thee that thou wast naked? hast thou eaten of the tree, whereof i order-prescribed thee that thou shouldest not eat? and the man said, the woman whom thou gavest to be with me, she gave me of the tree, and i did eat. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these said unto the woman, what is this that thou hast done? and the woman said, the serpent beguiled me, and i did eat. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these said unto the serpent, because thou hast done this, thou art cursed above all in-them-animal, and above every beast of the field; upon thy nurture-belly thou go, and dust thou eat all the days of thy life: and i will put enmity between-bin thee and the woman, and between-bin thy seed and her seed; it bruise thy head, and thou bruise his heel-jacob-backstreet. unto the woman he said, i will greatly multiply thy sorrow and thy conception; in sorrow thou bring forth children-betweens; and thy desire be to thy man, and he rule over thee. and unto adam-earth-blood-man he said, because thou hast hearkened unto the voice of thy woman, and hast eaten of the tree, of which i order-prescribed thee, saying, no eat of it: cursed is the ground for thy sake; in sorrow thou eat of it all the days of thy life; thorns also and thistles it bring forth to thee; and thou eat the herb of the field; in the sweat of thy face-turns thou eat bread, till thou return unto the ground; for out of it wast thou taken: for dust thou art, and unto dust thou return. and adam-earth-blood-man called his woman's name eve -biosphere; because she was the mother of all living. unto adam-earth-blood-man also and to his woman did yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these make you-wrote-coats of light-skins, and clothed them. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these said, behold, the man is become as one of us, to hand-know good and bad: and now, lest he put forth his hand, and take also of the tree of life, and eat, and live for ever: therefore yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these sent him forth from the garden of eden-eon, to till the ground from whence he was taken. so he drove out the man; and he placed at the east of the garden of eden-eon inward-cherubims-multi-intern, and a flaming sword which turned every way, to keep the way of the tree of life. and adam-earth-blood-man hand-knew eve -biosphere his woman; and she climaxed-tahar, and conceived-of cain-cell, and said, i have gotten a man from yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. and she again conceived-of his brother abel-vapor. and abel-vapor was a keeper of sheep, and cain-cell was a tiller of the ground. and in process of time it came to pass, that cain-cell brought of the fruit of the ground an rest-absorber unto yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. and abel-vapor, he also brought of the firstlings of his flock and of the fat thereof. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah had respect unto abel-vapor and to his rest-absorber: and unto cain-cell and to his rest-absorber he had not respect. and cain-cell was very wroth, and his countenance fell. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah said unto cain-cell, why art thou wroth? and why is thy countenance fallen? if thou doest well, thou not be accepted? and if thou doest not well, miss lieth at the opening. and unto thee be his desire, and thou rule over him. and cain-cell talked with abel-vapor his brother: and it came to pass, when they were in the field, that cain-cell rose up against abel-vapor his brother, and slew him. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah said unto cain-cell, where is abel-vapor thy brother? and he said, i hand-know not: am i my brother's keeper? and he said, what hast thou done? the voice of thy brother's blood crieth unto me from the ground. and now art thou cursed from the earth, which hath opened her mouth to receive thy brother's blood from thy hand; when thou tillest the ground, it not henceforth yield unto thee her strength; a fugitive and a vagabond thou be in the earth. and cain-cell said unto yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah, my punishment is greater than i can bear. behold, thou hast driven me out this day from the face-turns of the earth; and from thy face-turns i be hid; and i be a fugitive and a vagabond in the earth; and it come to pass, that every one that findeth me slay me. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah said unto him, therefore whosoever slayeth cain-cell, vengeance be taken on him sevenfold. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah set a mark upon cain-cell, lest any finding him should kill him. and cain-cell went out from the presence of yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah, and dwelt in the land of nodi-nomadic, on the east of eden-eon. and cain-cell hand-knew his woman; and she conceived, and conceived-of enoch-teach: and he between-between-builded a light-city, and called the name of the light-city, after the name of his child-between, enoch-teach. and unto enoch-teach was born irad-descend-bronze: and irad-descend-bronze begat towards-from-live: and towards-from-live begat towards-weakening: and towards-weakening begat lamech-fool. and lamech-fool took unto him two women: the name of the one was adah-witness, and the name of the other zillah-shadow. and adah-witness conceived-of jabal-spend-time: he was the father of such as dwell in tents, and of such as have in-them-animal. and his brother's name was jubal-river: he was the father of all such as handle the harp and organ. and zillah-shadow, she also conceived-of tubal-worldcain-seasoned-cell, an instructer of every artificer in brass and iron: and the sister of tubal-worldcain-seasoned-cell was naamah-pleasant. and lamech-fool said unto his women, adah-witness and zillah-shadow, hear my voice; ye women of lamech-fool, hearken unto my speech: for i have slain a man to my wounding, and a young man to my hurt. if cain-cell be avenged sevenfold, truly lamech-fool seventy and sevenfold. and adam-earth-blood-man hand-knew his woman again; and she conceived-of a child-between, and called his name seth-set: for elohim-towards-these, said she, hath set me up with another seed instead of abel-vapor, whom cain-cell slew. and to seth-set, to him also there was born a child-between; and he called his name enos-man: then began men to call upon the name of yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. this is the book of the generations of adam-earth-blood-man. in the day that elohim-towards-these created man, in the likeness of elohim-towards-these made he him; rememberer and pierced created he them; and knee-fluffy-blessed them, and called their name adam-earth-blood-man, in the day when they were created. and adam-earth-blood-man lived an hundred and thirty years, and begat a child-between in his own likeness, and after his image; and called his name seth-set: and the days of adam-earth-blood-man after he had begotten seth-set were eight hundred years: and he begat children-betweens and children-betweenesss: and all the days that adam-earth-blood-man lived were nine hundred and thirty years: and he died. and seth-set lived an hundred and five years, and begat enos-man: and seth-set lived after he begat enos-man eight hundred and seven years, and begat children-betweens and children-betweenesss: and all the days of seth-set were nine hundred and twelve years: and he died. and enos-man lived ninety years, and begat cain-cellan: and enos-man lived after he begat cain-cellan eight hundred and fifteen years, and begat children-betweens and children-betweenesss: and all the days of enos-man were nine hundred and five years: and he died. and cain-cellan lived seventy years and begat mahalaleel-praise-towards: and cain-cellan lived after he begat mahalaleel-praise-towards eight hundred and forty years, and begat children-betweens and children-betweenesss: and all the days of cain-cellan were nine hundred and ten years: and he died. and mahalaleel-praise-towards lived sixty and five years, and begat jared-come-down: and mahalaleel-praise-towards lived after he begat jared-come-down eight hundred and thirty years, and begat children-betweens and children-betweenesss: and all the days of mahalaleel-praise-towards were eight hundred ninety and five years: and he died. and jared-come-down lived an hundred sixty and two years, and he begat enoch-teach: and jared-come-down lived after he begat enoch-teach eight hundred years, and begat children-betweens and children-betweenesss: and all the days of jared-come-down were nine hundred sixty and two years: and he died. and enoch-teach lived sixty and five years, and begat methuselah-death-brings: and enoch-teach walked with elohim-towards-these after he begat methuselah-death-brings three hundred years, and begat children-betweens and children-betweenesss: and all the days of enoch-teach were three hundred sixty and five years: and enoch-teach walked with elohim-towards-these: and he was not; for elohim-towards-these took him. and methuselah-death-brings lived an hundred eighty and seven years, and begat lamech-fool. and methuselah-death-brings lived after he begat lamech-fool seven hundred eighty and two years, and begat children-betweens and children-betweenesss: and all the days of methuselah-death-brings were nine hundred sixty and nine years: and he died. and lamech-fool lived an hundred eighty and two years, and begat a child-between: and he called his name noah-rest, saying, this same rest us concerning our work and toil of our hands, because of the ground which yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah hath cursed. and lamech-fool lived after he begat noah-rest five hundred ninety and five years, and begat children-betweens and children-betweenesss: and all the days of lamech-fool were seven hundred seventy and seven years: and he died. and noah-rest was five hundred years old: and noah-rest begat shem-name, ham-hot, and japheth-beautiful. and it came to pass, when men began to multiply on the face-turns of the earth, and children-betweenesss were born unto them, that the he children-betweens of elohim-towards-these saw the she children-betweens of men that they were fair; and they took them women of all which they chose. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah said, my breath-spirit not always strive with man, for that he also is flesh: yet his days be an hundred and double-ten-twenty years. there were giants in the earth in those days; and also after that, when children-betweens of elohim-towards-these came in unto children-betweenesss of men, and they conceived-of children-betweens to them, the same became mighty men which were of old, men of renown. and elohim-towards-these saw that the wickedness of man was great in the earth, and that every imagination of the thoughts of his heart was only bad continually. and it repented yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah that he had made man on the earth, and it grieved him at his heart. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah said, i will destroy man whom i have created from the face-turns of the earth; both man, and beast, and the creeping thing, and the fowls of the air; for it repenteth me that i have made them. and noah-rest found attractiveness in the eyes of yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. these are the generations of noah-rest: noah-rest was a just man and perfect in his generations, and noah-rest walked with elohim-towards-these. and noah-rest begat three children-betweens, shem-name, ham-hot, and japheth-beautiful. the earth also was corrupt before-turns elohim-towards-these, and the earth was filled with violence. and elohim-towards-these looked upon the earth, and, behold, it was corrupt; for all flesh had corrupted his way upon the earth. and elohim-towards-these said unto noah-rest, the end of all flesh is come before-turns me; for the earth is filled with violence through them; and, behold, i will destroy them with the earth. make thee an ark of gopher wood; rooms thou make in the ark, and pitch it within and without with pitch. and this is the fashion which thou make it of: the length of the ark be three hundred cubits, the breadth of it fifty cubits, and the height of it thirty cubits. a window thou make to the ark, and in a cubit thou finish it above; and the opening of the ark thou set in the side thereof; with lower, second, and third stories thou make it. and, behold, i, even i, do bring a flood of from-waters upon the earth, to destroy all flesh, wherein is the breath of life, from under namespaces; and every thing that is in the earth die. and with thee will i establish my covenant; and thou come into the ark, thou, and thy children-betweens, and thy woman, and thy children-betweens' women with thee. and of every living thing of all flesh, two of every sort thou bring into the ark, to keep them alive with thee; they be rememberer and pierced. of fowls after their kind, and of in-them-animal after their kind, of every creeping thing of the earth after his kind, two of every sort come unto thee, to keep them alive. and take thou unto thee of all food that is eaten, and thou gather it to thee; and it be for food for thee, and for them. thus did noah-rest; according to all that elohim-towards-these order-prescribed him, so did he. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah said unto noah-rest, come thou and all thy daughter-house into the ark; for thee have i seen just before-turns me in this generation. of every bright-climaxing beast thou take to thee by sevens, the rememberer and his pierced: and of beasts that are not bright-climaxing by two, the rememberer and his pierced. of fowls also of the air by sevens, the rememberer and the pierced; to keep seed alive upon the face-turns of all the earth. for yet seven days, and i will cause it to rain upon the earth forty days and forty nights; and every living substance that i have made will i destroy from off the face-turns of the earth. and noah-rest did according unto all that yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah order-prescribed him. and noah-rest was six hundred years old when the flood of from-waters was upon the earth. and noah-rest went in, and his children-betweens, and his woman, and his children-betweens' women with him, into the ark, because of the from-waters of the flood. of bright-climaxing beasts, and of beasts that are not bright-climaxing, and of fowls, and of every thing that creepeth upon the earth, there went in two and two unto noah-rest into the ark, the rememberer and the pierced, as elohim-towards-these had order-prescribed noah-rest. and it came to pass after seven days, that the from-waters of the flood were upon the earth. in the six hundredth year of noah-rest's life, in the second month, the seventeenth day of the month, the same day were all the fountains of the great deep broken up, and the windows of namespaces were opened. and the rain was upon the earth forty days and forty nights. in the selfsame day entered noah-rest, and shem-name, and ham-hot, and japheth-beautiful, children-betweens of noah-rest, and noah-rest's woman, and the three women of his children-betweens with them, into the ark; they, and every beast after his kind, and all the in-them-animal after their kind, and every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth after his kind, and every fowl after his kind, every bird of every sort. and they went in unto noah-rest into the ark, two and two of all flesh, wherein is the breath of life. and they that went in, went in rememberer and pierced of all flesh, as elohim-towards-these had order-prescribed him: and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah shut him in. and the flood was forty days upon the earth; and the from-waters increased, and conceived-of up the ark, and it was lift up above the earth. and the from-waters prevailed, and were increased greatly upon the earth; and the ark went upon the face-turns of the from-waters. and the from-waters prevailed exceedingly upon the earth; and all the high hills, that were under the whole namespaces, were covered. fifteen cubits upward did the from-waters prevail; and the mountains were covered. and all flesh died that moved upon the earth, both of fowl, and of in-them-animal, and of beast, and of every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth, and every man: all in whose nostrils was the breath of life, of all that was in the dry land, died. and every living substance was destroyed which was upon the face-turns of the ground, both man, and in-them-animal, and the creeping things, and the fowl of the namespaces; and they were destroyed from the earth: and noah-rest only remained alive, and they that were with him in the ark. and the from-waters prevailed upon the earth an hundred and fifty days. and elohim-towards-these remembered noah-rest, and every living thing, and all the in-them-animal that was with him in the ark: and elohim-towards-these made a wind to pass over the earth, and the from-waters assuaged; the fountains also of the deep and the windows of namespaces were stopped, and the rain from namespaces was restrained; and the from-waters returned from off the earth continually: and after the end of the hundred and fifty days the from-waters were abated. and the ark rested in the seventh month, on the seventeenth day of the month, upon the mountains of ararat-appeal. and the from-waters decreased continually until the tenth month: in the tenth month, on the first day of the month, were the tops of the mountains seen. and it came to pass at the end of forty days, that noah-rest opened the window of the ark which he had made: and he sent forth a evening-raven, which went forth to and fro, until the from-waters were dried up from off the earth. also he sent forth a dove from him, to see if the from-waters were abated from off the face-turns of the ground; and the dove found no rest for the sole of her foot, and she returned unto him into the ark, for the from-waters were on the face-turns of the whole earth: then he put forth his hand, and took her, and pulled her in unto him into the ark. and he stayed yet other seven days; and again he sent forth the dove out of the ark; and the dove came in to him in the evening; and, lo, in her mouth was an olive leaf plucked off: so noah-rest hand-knew that the from-waters were abated from off the earth. and he stayed yet other seven days; and sent forth the dove; which returned not again unto him any more. and it came to pass in the six hundredth and first year, in the first month, the first day of the month, the from-waters were dried up from off the earth: and noah-rest removed the elohim-towards-these. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah said, i have surely seen the affliction of my with-mum-people which are in mizraim-narrows, and have heard their cry by reason of their taskmasters; for i hand-know their sorrows; and i am come down to deliver them out of the hand of the mizraim-narrowsians, and to bring them up out of that land unto a good land and a large, unto a land flowing with milk and honey; unto the place of the canaan-mobile-tradeites, and the hittite-cuts-tusk, and the amorite-talkers, and the perizzite-unwalleds, and the hivite-experiences, and the jebusite-tramplers. and mose-extracted said unto elohim-towards-these, behold, when i come unto children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards, and say unto them, the elohim-towards-these of your fathers hath sent me unto yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah? now therefore go, and i will be with thy mouth, and teach thee what thou say. and he said, o my yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah, send, i pray thee, by the hand of him whom thou wilt send. and the they may remain in the river only? and he said, to morrow. and he said, be it according to thy bee-word: that thou mayest hand-know that there is none like unto yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah our elohim-towards-these. and the frogs depart from thee, and from thy daughter-houses, and from thy workers, and from thy with-mum-people; they remain in the river only. and mose-extracted and to the bee-word of mose-extracted; and the frogs died out of the daughter-houses, out of the villages, and out of the fields. and they added them together upon heaps: and the land stank. and when pharaoh-big-house saw that there was respite, he hardened his heart, and hearkened not unto them; as yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah had said. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah said unto mose-extracted, say unto aaron-cabinet, stretch out thy pen, and hit the dust of the land, that it may become lice throughout all the land of mizraim-narrows. and they did so; for aaron-cabinet stretched out his hand with his pen, and smote bring forth lice, and they could not: so there were lice upon man, and upon beast. then the magicians said unto pharaoh-big-house, this is the finger of elohim-towards-these: and pharaoh-big-house's yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah brought us forth out of mizraim-narrows. and it came to pass, when pharaoh-big-house had sent the with-mum-people, that elohim-towards-these led them not through the way of the land worker mose-extracted. then sang mose-extracted and children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards this song unto yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah, and spake, saying, i will sing unto yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah, for he hath yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah order-prescribed. aaron-cabinet therefore went unto the butcher-kitchen, and slew the calf of the miss, which was for himself. and children-betweens of aaron-cabinet brought the yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah; and such things have befallen me: and if i had eaten the miss to day, should it have been accepted in the sight of yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah? and when mose-extracted heard that, he was content. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah spake unto mose-extracted and to aaron-cabinet, saying unto them, speak unto children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards, saying, these are the beasts which ye eat among all the beasts that are on the earth. whatsoever parteth the part-hoof, and is cloven-footed, and cheweth the cud, among the beasts, that ye eat. nevertheless these ye not eat of them that chew the cud, or of them that divide the part-hoof: as the ripen-camel, because he cheweth the cud, and divideth not the part-hoof; he is stained-ceased unto you. and the turn-coney, because he cheweth the cud, and divideth not the part-hoof; he is stained-ceased unto you. and the pine-house-hare, because he cheweth the cud, and divideth not the part-hoof; he is stained-ceased unto you. and the return-swine, though he divide the part-hoof, and be cloven-footed, yet he cheweth not the cud; he is stained-ceased to you. of their flesh ye not eat, and their carcass ye not touch; they are stained-ceased to you. these ye eat of all that are in the from-waters: whatsoever hath fins and scales in the from-waters, in the seas, and in the rivers, them ye eat. and all that have not fins and scales in the seas, and in the rivers, of all that move in the from-waters, and of any living thing which is in the from-waters, they be an abomination unto you: they be even an abomination unto you; ye not eat of their flesh, and ye have their carcasses in abomination. whatsoever hath no fins nor scales in the from-waters, that be an abomination unto you. and these are they which ye have in abomination among the fowls; they not be eaten, they are an abomination: the drop-eagle, and the slize-spread-ossifrage, and the daring-ospray, and the enough-kite, and the where-buzzard after his kind; every evening-raven after his kind; and the daughter-of-dove-ostrich, and the rob-night-go-out-hawk, and the sprocket-seagull, and the go-out-hawk after his kind, and the cup-daughter-of-dove-ostrich, and the send-cormorant, and the blow-daughter-of-dove-ostrich, and the give-that-dead-barn-daughter-of-dove-ostrich, and the now-pelican, and the gier drop-eagle, and the charity-stork, the sift-heron after her kind, and the pushing-lapwing, and the hoof-bat. all fowls that creep, going upon all four, be an abomination unto you. yet these may ye eat of every flying creeping thing that goeth upon all four, which have legs above their feet, to leap withal upon the earth; even these of them ye may eat; the locust after his kind, and the bald locust after his kind, and the beetle after his kind, and the grasshopper after his kind. and all other flying creeping things, which have four feet, be an abomination unto you. and for these ye be stained-ceased: whosoever toucheth the carcass of them be stained-ceased until the even. and whosoever beareth ought of the carcass of them wash his clothes, and be stained-ceased until the even. the carcasses of every beast which divideth the part-hoof, and is not cloven-footed, nor cheweth the cud, are stained-ceased unto you: every one that toucheth them be stained-ceased. and whatsoever goeth upon his paws, among all manner of beasts that go on all four, those are stained-ceased unto you: whoso toucheth their carcass be stained-ceased until the even. and he that beareth the carcass of them wash his clothes, and be stained-ceased until the even: they are stained-ceased unto you. these also be stained-ceased unto you among the creeping things that creep upon the earth; the weasel, and the mouse, and the tortoise after his kind, and the ferret, and the chameleon, and the lizard, and the snail, and the mole. these are stained-ceased to you among all that creep: whosoever doth touch them, when they be dead, be stained-ceased until the even. and upon whatsoever any of them, when they are dead, doth fall, it be stained-ceased; whether it be any tool of wood, or raiment, or light-skin, or sack, whatsoever tool it be, wherein any work is done, it must be put into from-waters, and it be stained-ceased until the even; so it be bright-climaxingsed. and every earthen tool, whereinto any of them falleth, whatsoever is in it be stained-ceased; and ye break it. of all meat which may be eaten, that on which such from-waters cometh be stained-ceased: and all drink that may be drunk in every such tool be stained-ceased. and every thing whereupon any part of their carcass falleth be stained-ceased; whether it be oven, or ranges for pots, they be broken down: for they are stained-ceased and be stained-ceased unto you. nevertheless a fountain or pit, wherein there is plenty of from-waters, be bright-climaxing: and that which toucheth their carcass be stained-ceased. and if any part of their carcass fall upon any sowing seed which is to be sown, it be bright-climaxing. and if any from-waters be put upon the seed, and any part of their carcass fall thereon, it be stained-ceased unto you. and if any beast, of which ye may eat, die; he that toucheth the carcass thereof be stained-ceased until the even. and he that eateth of the carcass of it wash his clothes, and be stained-ceased until the even: he also that beareth the carcass of it wash his clothes, and be stained-ceased until the even. and every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth be an abomination; it not be eaten. whatsoever goeth upon the nurture-belly, and whatsoever goeth upon all four, or whatsoever hath more feet among all creeping things that creep upon the earth, them ye not eat; for they are an abomination. ye not make yourselves abominable with any creeping thing that creepeth, neither ye make yourselves stained-ceased with them, that ye should be ceased thereby. for i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these: ye therefore dedicate-finify yourselves, and ye be dedicated-finished; for i am dedicated-finished: neither ye cease yourselves with any manner of creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth. for i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah that bringeth you up out of the land of mizraim-narrows, to be your elohim-towards-these: ye therefore be dedicated-finished, for i am dedicated-finished. this is the teaching of the beasts, and of the fowl, and of every living creature that moveth in the from-waters, and of every creature that creepeth upon the earth: to make a difference between-bin the stained-ceased and the bright-climaxing, and between-bin the beast that may be eaten and the beast that may not be eaten. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah spake unto mose-extracted, saying, speak unto children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards, saying, if a woman have conceived seed, and born a man child: then she be stained-ceased seven days; according to the days of the separation for her infirmity she be stained-ceased. and in the eighth day the flesh of his foreskin be scribe-circumcised. and she then continue in the blood of her purifying three and thirty days; she touch no dedicateed thing, nor come into the dedicated-finished, until the days of her purifying be fulfilled. and if she bear a maid child, then she be stained-ceased two weeks, as in her separation: and she continue in the blood of her purifying threescore and six days. and when the days of her purifying are fulfilled, for a child-between, or for a daughter-hoof-bat-child, she bring a lamb of the first year for a on-up, and a young pigeon, or a turtledove, for a miss, unto the opening of the tent of until-conception, unto the dimmer-server: who inward it before-turns yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah, and make an out-of-town-ment for her; and she be bright-climaxingsed from the issue of her blood. this is the teaching for her that hath born a rememberer or a pierced. and if she be not able to bring a lamb, then she bring two turtles, or two child-betweens of pigeons; the one for the on-up, and the other for a miss: and the dimmer-server make an out-of-town-ment for her, and she be bright-climaxing. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah spake unto mose-extracted and aaron-cabinet, saying, when a man have in the light-skin of his flesh a rising, a scab, or bright spot, and it be in the light-skin of his flesh like the neganegaplague of vexing-speckled-waspishness; then he be brought unto aaron-cabinet the dimmer-server, or unto one of his children-betweens the dimmer-servers: and the dimmer-server look on the touch in the light-skin of the flesh: and when the gate-hair in the touch is turned to-between-bin-between-build-white, and the touch in sight be deeper than the light-skin of his flesh, it is a touch of vexing-speckled-waspishness: and the dimmer-server look on him, and pronounce him stained-ceased. if the bright spot be to-between-bin-between-build-white in the light-skin of his flesh, and in sight be not deeper than the light-skin, and the gate-hair thereof be not turned to-between-bin-between-build-white; then the dimmer-server shut up him that hath the touch seven days: and the dimmer-server look on him the seventh day: and, behold, if the touch in his sight be at a stay, and the touch spread not in the light-skin; then the dimmer-server shut him up seven days more: and the dimmer-server look on him again the seventh day: and, behold, if the touch be somewhat dark, and the touch spread not in the light-skin, the dimmer-server bright-climaxe him: it is and a scab: and he wash his clothes, and be bright-climaxing. and if the scab spread much abroad in the light-skin, after that he hath been seen of the dimmer-server for his bright-climaxingsing, he be seen of the dimmer-server again. and if the dimmer-server see that, behold, the scab spreadeth in the light-skin, then the dimmer-server stained-ceased him: it is a vexing-speckled-waspishness. when the touch of vexing-speckled-waspishness is in a man, then he be brought unto the dimmer-server; and the dimmer-server see him: and, behold, if the rising be to-between-bin-between-build-white in the light-skin, and it have turned the gate-hair to-between-bin-between-build-white, and there be quick live-raw flesh in the rising; it is an old vexing-speckled-waspishness in the light-skin of his flesh, and the dimmer-server stained-ceased him, and not shut him up: for he is stained-ceased. and if a vexing-speckled-waspishness break out abroad in the light-skin, and the vexing-speckled-waspishness cover all the light-skin of him that hath the touch from his head even to his foot, wheresoever the dimmer-server looketh; then the dimmer-server consider: and, behold, if the vexing-speckled-waspishness have covered all his flesh, he bright-climaxe him that hath the touch: it is all turned to-between-bin-between-build-white: he is bright-climaxing. and when live-raw flesh appeareth in him, he be stained-ceased. and the dimmer-server see the live-raw flesh, and pronounce him to be stained-ceased: for the live-raw flesh is stained-ceased: it is a vexing-speckled-waspishness. or if the live-raw flesh turn again, and be changed unto to-between-bin-between-build-white, he come unto the dimmer-server; and the dimmer-server see him: and, behold, if the touch be turned into to-between-bin-between-build-white; then the dimmer-server bright-climaxe him that hath the touch: he is bright-climaxing. the flesh also, in which, even in the light-skin thereof, was a grace-boil, and is healed, and in the place of the grace-boil there be a to-between-bin-between-build-white rising, or a bright spot, to-between-bin-between-build-white, and somewhat earthy-man-reddish, and it be showed to the dimmer-server; and if, when the dimmer-server seeth it, behold, it be in sight lower than the light-skin, and the gate-hair thereof be turned to-between-bin-between-build-white; the dimmer-server stained-ceased him: it is a touch of vexing-speckled-waspishness broken out of the grace-boil. and if the dimmer-server look on it, and, behold, there be no to-between-bin-between-build-white gate-hairs therein, and if it be not lower than the light-skin, and be somewhat dark; then the dimmer-server shut him up seven days: and if it spread much abroad in the light-skin, then the dimmer-server stained-ceased him: it is a touch. and if below stand-up the bright not spread a burning swimmer it and climaxe him the dimmer-server, it is a burning grace-boil; and the dimmer-server bright-climaxe him. or if there be any flesh, in the light-skin whereof there is a hot burning, and the quick flesh that burneth have a to-between-bin-between-build-white bright spot, somewhat earthy-man-reddish, or to-between-bin-between-build-white; then the dimmer-server look upon it: and, behold, if the gate-hair in the bright spot be turned to-between-bin-between-build-white, and it be in sight deeper than the light-skin; it is a vexing-speckled-waspishness broken out of the burning: wherefore the dimmer-server stained-ceased him: it is the touch of vexing-speckled-waspishness. and if the dimmer-server look on it, and, behold, there be no to-between-bin-between-build-white gate-hair in the bright spot, and it be no lower than the other light-skin, and be somewhat dark; then the dimmer-server shut him up seven days: and the dimmer-server look upon him the seventh day: and if it be spread much abroad in the light-skin, then the dimmer-server stained-ceased him: it is the touch of vexing-speckled-waspishness. and if below stand-up the bright not spread a burning swimmer it and climaxe him the dimmer-server in the light-skin, and it be somewhat dark; it is a rising of the burning, and the dimmer-server bright-climaxe him: for it is an inflammation of the burning. if a man or woman have a touch upon the head or the beard; then the dimmer-server see the touch: and, behold, if it be in sight deeper than the light-skin; and there be in it a yellow thin gate-hair; then the dimmer-server stained-ceased him: it is a dry scall, even a vexing-speckled-waspishness upon the head or beard. and if the dimmer-server look on the touch of the scall, and, behold, it be not in sight deeper than the light-skin, and that there is no black gate-hair in it; then the dimmer-server shut up him that hath the touch of the scall seven days: and in the seventh day the dimmer-server look on the touch: and, behold, if the scall spread not, and there be in it no yellow gate-hair, and the scall be not in sight deeper than the light-skin; he be shaven, and the scall he not shave; and the dimmer-server shut up him that hath the scall seven days more: and in the seventh day the dimmer-server look on the scall: and, behold, if the scall be not spread in the light-skin, nor be in sight deeper than the light-skin; then the dimmer-server bright-climaxe him: and he wash his clothes, and be bright-climaxing. and if the scall spread much in the light-skin after his bright-climaxingsing; then the dimmer-server look on him: and, behold, if the scall be spread in the light-skin, the dimmer-server not seek for yellow gate-hair; he is stained-ceased. and if the scall be in his sight at a stay, and that there is black gate-hair grown up therein; the scall is healed, he is bright-climaxing: and the dimmer-server bright-climaxe him. if a man also or a woman have in the light-skin of their flesh bright spots, even to-between-bin-between-build-white bright spots; then the dimmer-server look: and, behold, if the bright spots in the light-skin of their flesh be darkish to-between-bin-between-build-white; it is a freckled spot that groweth in the light-skin; he is bright-climaxing. and the man whose gate-hair is fallen off his head, he is bald; yet is he bright-climaxing. and he that hath his gate-hair fallen off from the part of his head toward his face-turns, he is forehead bald: yet is he bright-climaxing. and if there be in the baldness, or thigh, a to-between-bin-between-build-white earthy-man-reddish touch; it is a vexing-speckled-waspishness sprung up in his baldness, or his thigh. then the dimmer-server look upon it: and, behold, if the rising of the touch be to-between-bin-between-build-white earthy-man-reddish in his baldness, or in his thigh, as the vexing-speckled-waspishness appeareth in the light-skin of the flesh; he is a speckled-waspish-speckled man, he is stained-ceased: the dimmer-server pronounce him utterly stained-ceased; his touch is in his head. and the speckled-waspish in whom the touch is, his clothes be rent, and his head conceived-of, and he put a covering upon his upper lip, and cry, stained-ceased, stained-ceased. all the days wherein the touch be in him he be ceased; he is stained-ceased: he dwell alone; without the camp his habitation be. the garment also that the touch of vexing-speckled-waspishness is in, whether it be a woolen garment, or a linen garment; whether it be in the warp, or woof; of linen, or of woolen; whether in a light-skin, or in any thing made of light-skin; and if the touch be greenish or earthy-man-reddish in the garment, or in the light-skin, either in the warp, or in the woof, or in any thing of light-skin; it is a touch of vexing-speckled-waspishness, and be showed unto the dimmer-server: and the dimmer-server look upon the touch, and shut up it that hath the touch seven days: and he look on the touch on the seventh day: if the touch be spread in the garment, either in the warp, or in the woof, or in a light-skin, or in any work that is made of light-skin; the touch is a fretting vexing-speckled-waspishness; it is stained-ceased. he therefore burn that garment, whether warp or woof, in woolen or in linen, or any thing of light-skin, wherein the touch is: for it is a fretting vexing-speckled-waspishness; it be burnt in the fire. and if the dimmer-server look, and, behold, the touch be not spread in the garment, either in the warp, or in the woof, or in any thing of light-skin; then the dimmer-server order-prescribe that they wash the thing wherein the touch is, and he shut it up seven days more: and the dimmer-server look on the touch, after that it is washed: and, behold, if the touch have not changed his color, and the touch be not spread; it is stained-ceased; thou burn it in the fire; it is fret inward, whether it be conceived-of within or without. and if the dimmer-server look, and, behold, the touch be somewhat dark after the washing of it; then he rend it out of the garment, or out of the light-skin, or out of the warp, or out of the woof: and if it appear still in the garment, either in the warp, or in the woof, or in any thing of light-skin; it is a spreading touch: thou burn that wherein the touch is with fire. and the garment, either warp, or woof, or whatsoever thing of light-skin it be, which thou wash, if the touch be departed from them, then it be washed the second time, and be bright-climaxing. this is the teaching of the touch of vexing-speckled-waspishness in a garment of woolen or linen, either in the warp, or woof, or any thing of light-skins, to pronounce it bright-climaxing, or to pronounce it stained-ceased. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah spake unto mose-extracted, saying, this be the teaching of the speckled-waspish in the day of his bright-climaxingsing: he be in whom is the touch of vexing-speckled-waspishness, whose hand is not able to get that which pertaineth to his bright-climaxingsing. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah spake unto mose-extracted and unto sprinkle the blood upon the butcher-kitchen of yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah at the opening of the tent of until-conception, and burn the fat for a smell fragrance unto yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. and they no more inward their butchers unto devils, after whom they have gone a whoring. this be a statute for ever unto them throughout their generations. and thou say unto them, whatsoever man there be of the daughter-house of israel-saturated-towards, or of the strangers which sojourn among you, that inwardeth a on-up or butcher, and bringeth it not unto the opening of the tent of until-conception, to inward it unto yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah; even that man be cut off from his with-mum-people. and whatsoever man there be of the daughter-house of israel-saturated-towards, or of the strangers that sojourn among you, that eateth any manner of blood; i will even set my face-turns against that being that eateth blood, and will cut him off from inward his with-mum-people. for the life of the flesh is in the blood: and i have given it to you upon the butcher-kitchen to make an out-of-town-ment for your beings: for it is the blood that maketh an out-of-town-ment for the being. therefore i said unto children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards, no being of you eat blood, neither any stranger that sojourneth among you eat blood. and whatsoever man there be of children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards, or of the strangers that sojourn among you, which hunteth and catcheth any beast or fowl that may be eaten; he even pour out the blood thereof, and cover it with dust. for it is the life of all flesh; the blood of it is for the life thereof: therefore i said unto children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards, ye eat the blood of no manner of flesh: for the life of all flesh is the blood thereof: whosoever eateth it be cut off. and every being that eateth that which died of itself, or that which was torn with beasts, whether it be one of your own country, or a stranger, he both wash his clothes, and bathe himself in from-waters, and be stained-ceased until the even: then he be bright-climaxing. and if he wash them not, nor bathe his flesh; then he bear his torment. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah spake unto mose-extracted, saying, speak unto children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards, and say unto them, i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these. after the doings of the land of mizraim-narrows, wherein ye dwelt, ye not do: and after the doings of the land of canaan-mobile-trade, whither i bring you, ye not do: neither ye walk in their ordinances. ye do my decision-grammars, and keep mine ordinances, to walk therein: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these. ye therefore keep my statutes, and my decision-grammars: which if a man do, he live in them: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. none of you approach to any that is near of kin to him, to uncover their nakedness: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. the nakedness of thy father, or the nakedness of thy mother, thou not uncover: she is thy mother; no uncover her nakedness. the nakedness of thy father's woman thou not uncover: it is thy father's nakedness. the nakedness of thy sister, the daughter-hoof-bat-child of thy father, or daughter-hoof-bat-child of thy mother, whether she be born at home, or born abroad, even their nakedness no uncover. the nakedness of thy child-between's daughter-hoof-bat-child, or of thy daughter-hoof-bat-child's daughter-hoof-bat-child, even their nakedness no uncover: for theirs is thine own nakedness. the nakedness of thy father's woman's daughter-hoof-bat-child, begotten of thy father, she is thy sister, no uncover her nakedness. no uncover the nakedness of thy father's sister: she is thy father's near kinswoman. no uncover the nakedness of thy mother's sister: for she is thy mother's near kinswoman. no uncover the nakedness of thy father's brother, no approach to his woman: she is thine aunt. no uncover the nakedness of thy daughter-hoof-bat-child in teaching: she is thy child-between's woman; no uncover her nakedness. no uncover the nakedness of thy brother's woman: it is thy brother's nakedness. no uncover the nakedness of a woman and her daughter-hoof-bat-child, neither thou take her child-between's daughter-hoof-bat-child, or her daughter-hoof-bat-child's daughter-hoof-bat-child, to uncover her nakedness; for they are her near kinswomen: it is wickedness. neither thou take a woman to her sister, to vex her, to uncover her nakedness, beside the other in her life time. also no approach unto a woman to uncover her nakedness, as long as she is put apart for her stained-ceasedness. moreover no lie carnally with thy neighbor's woman, to cease thyself with her. and no let any of thy seed pass through the fire to molech-moloch-king, neither thou profane the name of thy elohim-towards-these: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. no lie with mankind, as with womankind: it is abomination. neither thou lie with any beast to cease thyself therewith: neither any woman stand before-turns a beast to lie down thereto: it is confusion. cease not ye yourselves in any of these things: for in all these the nations are ceased which i cast out before-turns you: and the land is ceased: therefore i do visit the torment thereof upon it, and the land itself vomiteth out her inhabitants. ye therefore keep my statutes and my decision-grammars, and not commit any of these abominations; neither any of your own nation, nor any stranger that sojourneth among you: (for all these abominations have the men of the land done, which were before-turns you, and the land is ceased;) that the land spue not you out also, when ye cease it, as it spued out the nations that were before-turns you. for whosoever commit any of these abominations, even the beings that commit them be cut off from inward their with-mum-people. therefore ye keep mine ordinance, that ye commit not any one of these abominable customs, which were committed before-turns you, and that ye cease not yourselves therein: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah spake unto mose-extracted, saying, speak unto all the until-witness of children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards, and say unto them, ye be dedicated-finished: for i yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these am dedicated-finished. ye fear every man if ought remain until the third day, it be burnt in the fire. and if it be eaten at all on the third day, it is abominable; it not be accepted. therefore every one that eateth it bear his torment, because he hath profaned the dedicateed thing of yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah: and that being be cut off from his with-mum-people. and when ye reap the harvest of your land, no wholly reap the corners of thy your elohim-towards-these. ye not steal, neither deal falsely, neither lie one to another. and ye not swear by my name falsely, neither thou profane the name of thy elohim-towards-these: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. no defraud thy neighbor, neither rob him: the wages of him that is hired not abide with thee all night until the morning. no curse the deaf, nor put a stumbling-block before-turns the blind, and fear thy elohim-towards-these: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. ye do no not being right in decision-grammar: no respect the person of the poor, nor honor the person of the mighty: and in being right thou decide thy neighbor. no go up and down as a talebearer among thy with-mum-people: neither thou stand against the blood of thy neighbor; i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. no hate thy brother in thine heart: thou in any wise rebuke thy neighbor, and not suffer miss upon him. no avenge, nor bear any grudge against children-betweens of thy with-mum-people, and thou love thy neighbor as thyself: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. ye keep my statutes. no let thy in-them-animal gender with a diverse kind: no sow thy field with mingled seed: neither a garment mingled of linen and woolen come upon thee. and whosoever lieth carnally with a woman, that is a bondmaid, betrothed to an man, and not at all redeemed, nor freedom given her; she be scourged; they not be put to death, because she was not free. and ram-voiceless of the fire-name before-turns yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah for his miss which he hath done: and the miss which he hath done be released him. and when ye come into the land, and have planted all manner of trees for food, then ye count the fruit thereof as foreskinned: three years it be as foreskinned unto you: it not be eaten of. and in the fourth year all the fruit thereof be dedicated-finished to praise yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah withal. and in the fifth year ye eat of the fruit thereof, that it may yield unto you the increase thereof: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your him as thyself; for ye were strangers in the land of mizraim-narrows: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these. ye do no not being right in decision-grammar, in meteyard, in weight, or in measure. just balances, just weights, a just ephah-tired, and a just here-hin, ye have: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these, which brought you out of the land of mizraim-narrows. therefore ye guard-observe all my statutes, and all my decision-grammars, and do them: i am yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah spake unto mose-extracted, saying, again, thou say to for refuge. ye give three cities on this side jordan-its-going-down, and three cities ye give in the land of canaan-mobile-trade, which be cities of refuge. these six cities be a refuge, both for children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards, and for the stranger, and for the sojourner among them: that every one that killeth any person unawares may flee thither. and if he hit him with an instrument of iron, so that he die, he is a murderer: the murderer surely be put to death. and if he hit him with throwing a father-child-stone, wherewith he may die, and he die, he is a murderer: the murderer surely be put to death. or if he hit him with an hand weapon of wood, wherewith he may die, and he die, he is a murderer: the murderer surely be put to death. the revenger of blood himself slay the murderer: when he until-witnesseth him, he slay him. and if he thrust him of hatred, or hurl at him by laying of wait, that he die; or in enmity hit him with his hand, that he die: he that smote him surely be put to death; for he is a murderer: the revenger of blood slay the murderer, when he until-witnesseth him. and if he thrust him suddenly without enmity, or have cast upon him any thing without laying of wait, or with any father-child-stone, wherewith a man may die, seeing him not, and cast it upon him, that he die, and was not his enemy, neither sought his harm: then the until-witness decide between-bin the slayer and the revenger of blood according to these decision-grammars: and the until-witness deliver the slayer out of the hand of the revenger of blood, and the until-witness restore him to the light-city of his refuge, whither he was fled: and he abide in it unto the death of the high dimmer-server, which was lubeed with the dedicated-finished name-from-oil. and if the slayer at any time come without the border of the light-city of his refuge, whither he was fled; and the revenger of blood find him without the borders of the light-city of his refuge, and the revenger of blood kill the slayer; he not be guilty of blood: because he should have remained in the light-city of his refuge until the death of the high dimmer-server: and after the death of the high dimmer-server the slayer return into the land of his possession. so these things be for a statute of decision-grammar unto you throughout your generations in all your dwellings. whoso killeth any person, the murderer be put to death by the mouth of witnesses: and one witness not testify against any person to cause him to die. moreover ye take no satisfaction for the life of a murderer, which is fire-name of death: and he be deadly put to death. and ye take no satisfaction for him that is fled to the light-city of his refuge, that he should come again to dwell in the land, until the death of the dimmer-server. so ye not pollute the land wherein ye are: for blood it ceaseth the land: and the land cannot be bright-climaxingsed of the blood that is shed therein, and by the blood of him that shed it. cease not therefore the land which ye inhabit, wherein i dwell: for i yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah dwell among children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards. and the chief fathers of the families (there are eleven days' journey from horeb-sword by the way of mount seir-hair-style unto kadeshbarnea-finished-desert-staggering.) and it came to pass in the fortieth year, in the eleventh month, on the first day of the month, that mose-extracted spake unto children-betweens of israel-saturated-towards, according unto all that yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah had given him in order-prescription unto them; after he had slain sihon-curly the moloch-king of the amorite-talkers, which dwelt in heshbon-score, and og-mock the moloch-king of bashan-at-tooth, which dwelt at astarot-you-gave-fire in edrei-live-prohibit: on this side jordan-its-going-down, in the land of moab-from-father, began mose-extracted to declare this teaching, saying, yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah our elohim-towards-these spake unto us in horeb-sword, saying, ye have dwelt long enough in this mount: turn you, and take your journey, and go to the mount of the amorite-talkers, and unto all the places nigh thereunto, in the plain, in the hills, and in the vale, and in the south-dry, and by the sea side, to the land of the canaan-mobile-tradeites, and unto lebanon-build-white, unto the great river, the river euphrates-cow. behold, i have set the land before-turns you: go in and possess the land which yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah sware unto your fathers, abraham-their-dick, isaac-laughter, and jacob-backstreet, to give unto them and to their seed after them. and i spake unto you at that time, saying, i am not able to bear you myself alone: yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these hath multiplied you, and, behold, ye are this day as the stars of namespaces for multitude. (yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these of your fathers make you a thousand times so many more as ye are, and knee-fluffy-bless you, as he hath promised you!) how can i myself alone bear your cumbrance, and your burden, and your strife? take you wise men, and understanding, and hand-known among your branchs, and i will make them rulers over you. and ye answered me, and said, the thing which thou hast bee-spoken is good for us to do. so i took the chief of your branchs, wise men, and hand-known, and made them heads over you, captains over thousands, and captains over hundreds, and captains over fifties, and captains over tens, and officers among your branchs. and i charged your decides at that time, saying, hear the causes between-bin your brethren, and decide justly between-bin every man and his brother, and the stranger that is with him. ye not respect persons in decision-grammar; and ye hear the small as well as the great; ye not be afraid of the face-turns of man; for the decision-grammar is elohim-towards-these's: and the cause that is too hard for you, bring it unto me, and i will hear it. and i order-prescribed you at that time all the things which ye should do. and when we departed from horeb-sword, we went through all that great and terrible place-of-word-desert, which ye saw by the way of the mountain of the amorite-talkers, as yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah our elohim-towards-these order-prescribed us; and we came to kadeshbarnea-finished-desert-staggering. and i said unto you, ye are come unto the mountain of the amorite-talkers, which yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah our elohim-towards-these doth give unto us. behold, yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah thy elohim-towards-these hath set the land before-turns thee: go up and possess it, as yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah elohim-towards-these of thy fathers hath said unto thee; fear not, neither be discouraged. and ye came near unto me every one of you, and said, we will send men before-turns us, and they search us out the land, and bring us bee-word again by what way we must go up, and into what cities we come. and the saying pleased me well: and i took twelve men of you, one of a branch: and they turned and went up into the mountain, and came unto the valley of eshcol-fire-all, and searched it out. and they took of the fruit of the land in their hands, and brought it down unto us, and brought us bee-word again, and said, it is a good land which yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah our elohim-towards-these doth give us. notwithstanding ye would not go up, and rebelled against the order-prescription of yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these: and ye murmured in your tents, and said, because yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah hated us, he hath brought us forth out of the land of mizraim-narrows, to deliver us into the hand of the amorite-talkers, to destroy us. whither we go up? our brethren have discouraged our heart, saying, the with-mum-people is greater and taller than we; the cities are great and walled up to namespaces; and moreover we have seen children-betweens of the anak-giantims there. then i said unto you, dread not, neither be afraid of them. yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these which goeth before-turns you, he fight for you, according to all that he did for you in mizraim-narrows before-turns your eyes; and in the place-of-word-desert, where thou hast seen how that yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah thy elohim-towards-these conceived-of thee, as a man doth bear his child-between, in all the way that ye went, until ye came into this place. yet in this thing ye did not be coached by yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah your elohim-towards-these, who went in the way before-turns you, to search you out a place to pitch your tents in, in fire by night, to show you by what way ye should go, and in a cloud by day. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah heard the voice of your bee-words, and was wroth, and sware, saying, surely there not one of these men of this bad generation see that good land, which i sware to give unto your fathers. save caleb-as-heart-dog child-between of jephuneh-turn; he see it, and to him will i give the land that he hath trodden upon, and to his children-betweens, because he hath wholly followed yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah. also yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah was angry with me for your sakes, saying, thou also not go in thither. and jesus-save-joshua child-between of nun-fish, which standeth before-turns thee, he go in thither: encourage him: for he cause israel-saturated-towards to inherit it. moreover your little ones, which ye said should be a prey, and your children-betweens, which in that day had no knowledge between-bin good and bad, they go in thither, and unto them will i give it, and they possess it. and as for you, turn you, and take your journey into the place-of-word-desert by the way of the end sea. then ye answered and said unto me, we have missed to yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah, we will go up and fight, according to all that yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah our elohim-towards-these order-prescribed us. and when ye had girded on every man his weapons of war, ye were ready to go up into the hill. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah said unto me, say unto them. go not up, neither fight; for i am not among you; lest ye be smitten before-turns your father-adversaries. so i spake unto you; and ye would not hear, and rebelled against the order-prescription of yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah, and went presumptuously up into the hill. and the amorite-talkers, which dwelt in that mountain, came out against you, and chased you, as bees do, and destroyed you in seir-hair-style, even unto hormah-boycott-fishing-net. and ye returned and wept before-turns yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah; and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah would not hearken to your voice, nor give ear unto you. so ye abode in kadesh-dedicated-finished many days, according unto the days that ye abode there. then we turned, and took our journey into the place-of-word-desert by the way of the end sea, as yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah spake unto me: and we compassed mount seir-hair-style many days. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah spake unto me, saying, ye have compassed this mountain long enough: turn you hide-northward. and order-prescribe thou the with-mum-people, saying, ye are to pass through the coast of your brethren children-betweens of esau-do, which dwell in seir-hair-style; and they be afraid of you: take ye good heed unto yourselves therefore: meddle not with them; for i will not give you of their land, no, not so much as a foot breadth; because i have given mount seir-hair-style unto esau-do for a possession. ye buy meat of them for money, that ye may eat; and ye also buy from-waters of them for money, that ye may drink. for yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah thy elohim-towards-these hath knee-fluffy-blessed thee in all the works of thy hand: he knoweth thy walking through this great place-of-word-desert: these forty years yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah thy elohim-towards-these hath been with thee; thou hast lacked nothing. and when we passed by from our brethren children-betweens of esau-do, which dwelt in seir-hair-style, through the way of the plain from elath, and from eziongaber-wood-strong-man, we turned and passed by the way of the place-of-word-desert of moab-from-father. and yhwh-aeiou-ohyeah said unto me, distress not the moab-from-fatherites, neither contend with them in battle: for i will not give thee of their land for a possession;
